--
-- Structure de la table `aauth_user_variables`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `aauth_user_variables`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `aauth_user_variables` (
  `id` int(11) UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` int(11) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `data_key` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `value` text,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `user_id_index` (`user_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la table `classe`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `classe`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `classe` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `idEnseignant` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `anneeScolaire` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `idNiveau` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `classe_fk_1` (`idEnseignant`),
  KEY `classe_fk_2` (`idNiveau`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=10 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

--
-- Déchargement des données de la table `classe`
--

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la table `comporter`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `comporter`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `comporter` (
  `idLivre` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `IdRallye` int(11) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`IdRallye`,`idLivre`),
  KEY `comporter_fk_1` (`idLivre`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

-- Structure de la table `editeur`

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `editeur`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `editeur` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `nom` varchar(60) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=133 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la table `question`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `question`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `question` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `question` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `points` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `idQuizz` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `fk_question_idQuizz` (`idQuizz`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=839 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la table `rallye`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `rallye`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `rallye` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `dateDebut` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `duree` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `theme` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la table `reponse`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `reponse`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `reponse` (
  `idQuestion` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `idProposition` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `idParticiperRallye` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `idParticiperEleve` int(11) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idQuestion`,`idProposition`,`idParticiperRallye`,`idParticiperEleve`),
  KEY `fk_reponse_idProposition` (`idProposition`),
  KEY `fk_reponse_idParticiperRallye` (`idParticiperRallye`),
  KEY `fk_reponse_idParticiperEleve` (`idParticiperEleve`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
COMMIT;
